msg:As expected of a four-star hotel with official national star certification, the service is absolutely amazing! When we checked in in the afternoon, the room the front desk gave us at first was not satisfactory because we could not see any exterior view due to the building itself. So we went back to the front desk to negotiate. We were originally going to cancel the order and find a new hotel, but the front desk guy upgraded us to a deluxe room for free without saying a word. What was even more surprising was that my family happened to have a birthday that day. When we went out to play for a while and returned to the room at night, there was a big birthday cake and a greeting card on the table! Some of our other requests were also met, and the room service staff were very friendly! A pleasant hotel experience!
In addition, the hotel is in a good location, with a bus stop at the door, and only 10 minutes away from Wuhu Railway Station and the nearest light rail station, making it very convenient to travel! I sincerely recommend it!
